Australian Government Disaster Recovery Payment (AGDRP) and New Zealand Disaster Recovery Payment (NZ DRP)

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU),   |
|                                   |     or                            |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud. For Pandemic Leave         |
|                                   | Disaster Payment potential fraud, |
|                                   | staff must report Fast Fraud      |
|                                   | Tip-off Form - Emergency          |
|                                   | Payments.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, Service Officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that has been finalised   |
|                                   | on a Multiple CRN, go to Step 5   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that is In Process on a   |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, go to Step 5        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the claim on the Multiple  |
|                                   | CRN + Read more ...               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Multiple CRN, identify the |
|                                   | AGDRP claim the customer          |
|                                   | submitted, using:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For online claims:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Transaction icon in Process   |
|                                   |     Direct (online claims), or    |
|                                   | -   Assisted Customer Claim icon  |
|                                   |     on the desktop                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For paper claims scanned to       |
|                                   | Documents, a blank Social Online  |
|                                   | Application (SOA) will be created |
|                                   | and assigned for processing:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Any personal information from |
|                                   |     the claim will need to be     |
|                                   |     updated on the customer's     |
|                                   |     record. For example, updating |
|                                   |     contact details               |
|                                   | -   Information from the paper    |
|                                   |     claim will need to be         |
|                                   |     transposed to the Disaster    |
|                                   |     Recovery claim screens in the |
|                                   |     SOA                           |
|                                   | -   Review the customers claim   |
|                                   |     following the steps below,    |
|                                   |     noting that information will  |
|                                   |     need to be recorded when      |
|                                   |     processing the claim          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identify any scanned documents    |
|                                   | used to assess this claim using:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First, or                     |
|                                   | -   as part of the claim bundle   |
|                                   |     under Transaction icon in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the following points in   |
|                                   | order to determine the            |
|                                   | remediation required.             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the multiple record:           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the Event to determine if |
|                                   | the claim has been completed:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   check the Payment Summary     |
|                                   |     screen (PS)                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the date of receipt. This |
|                                   | is the date the claim was         |
|                                   | submitted or scanned              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review any Identity Documents     |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Transfer information + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manually replicate any DOCs and   |
|                                   | Notes relevant to the claim onto  |
|                                   | the primary record                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Transfer any scanned documents    |
|                                   | lodged on the Multiple CRN since  |
|                                   | the original claim to the primary |
|                                   | record                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Print and scan Multiple CRN claim |
|                                   | onto Primary CRN:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Locate the Online Claim in    |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant hyperlink |
|                                   |     Claim ID for the Emergency    |
|                                   |     Payment                       |
|                                   | -   Select Claim Summary          |
|                                   | -   Print this online claim, save |
|                                   |     as pdf and upload to the      |
|                                   |     Primary CRN                   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Identity Confirmation Status +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the primary CRN have a       |
|                                   | confirmed Services Australia and  |

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Identity Confirmation Dashboard + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Multiple CRN have a      |
|                                   | Services Australia or Digital     |
|                                   | Identity confirmation status?     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   refer to Data Quality Unit -  |
|                                   |     Identity SME for remediation. |
|                                   |     See Resources for contact     |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   place the activity on hold    |
|                                   |     for 1 day to refer to Data    |
|                                   |     Quality Unit - Identity SME   |
|                                   |     for remediation. Upon         |
|                                   |     maturity of activity and/or   |
|                                   |     Identity Confirmation Status  |
|                                   |     remediation on primary CRN,   |
|                                   |     go to Step 10                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   does not have a confirmed     |
|                                   |     Services Australia identity,  |
|                                   |     code the Services Australia   |
|                                   |     identity documents from the   |
|                                   |     multiple CRNs to the primary  |
|                                   |     record via the Identity       |
|                                   |     Dashboard in Process Direct.  |
|                                   |     See Resources for the         |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN Identity         |
|                                   |     Remediation task card. Go to  |
|                                   |     Step 10                       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | AGDRP and NZ DRP In Process     |
|                                   | claims + Read more ...            |

|                                   | -   Annotate the Progress of      |
|                                   |     Claim note to record claim    |
|                                   |     lodged on multiple CRN and    |
|                                   |     processed on primary CRN      |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Staff must not select a       |
|                                   |     Disaster Recovery Payment     |
|                                   |     activity from the Activity    |
|                                   |     List (AL) screen in Customer  |
|                                   |     First. This is an associated  |
|                                   |     activity (as a result of      |
|                                   |     selecting the Assess button   |
|                                   |     in Process Direct), but it is |
|                                   |     not the claim activity.       |
|                                   |     Select claims from Process    |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers without !FFAP    |
|                                   | access:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Claims are to be assigned to      |
|                                   | staff with !FFAP access if the    |
|                                   | keyword NOM has been applied due  |
|                                   | to the following reasons:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   payment is to be issued to a  |
|                                   |     payment nominee, or           |
|                                   | -   NZ DRP claims include         |
|                                   |     secondary claimants (spouse,  |
|                                   |     dependent adult, and/or       |
|                                   |     non-dependent child who lives |
|                                   |     with them)                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To re-assign the claim to a       |
|                                   | Service Officer with !FFAP        |
|                                   | access, add the Keyword NOM       |

Covid-19 Disaster Payment

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud. For Covid-19 Disaster      |
|                                   | Payment potential fraud, staff    |
|                                   | must report Fast Fraud Tip-off    |
|                                   | Form - Emergency Payments.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, Service Officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a draft claim or a claim that has |
|                                   | been finalised on a Multiple CRN, |
|                                   | go to Step 5                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that is In Process on a   |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, go to Step 5        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |

| 18                                | Process the COVID-19 Disaster     |
|                                   | Payment Continuation Payment on   |
|                                   | Primary CRN + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer received a       |
|                                   | continuation payment on the       |
|                                   | Primary CRN and was this for the  |
|                                   | next Relevant Period based on the |
|                                   | last Relevant Period paid on the  |
|                                   | Multiple CRN?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, see Table 6                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the customer was paid      |
|                                   |     incorrectly and has been      |
|                                   |     overpaid on the Multiple CRN  |
|                                   |     and/or Primary CRN            |
|                                   |     The customer has received     |
|                                   |     payment for the same relevant |
|                                   |     period more than once on      |
|                                   |     either the Multiple CRN       |
|                                   |     and/or Primary CRN, go to     |
|                                   |     Step 17                       |
|                                   | -   If the customer has not been  |
|                                   |     paid from the next Relevant   |
|                                   |     Period. That is, there is a   |
|                                   |     gap (break) in payment from   |
|                                   |     the last Relevant Period paid |

|                                   |     Primary CRN                   |
|                                   |     Grant the continuation        |
|                                   |     payment for the Gap (break)   |
|                                   |     Relevant Period by running    |
|                                   |     the Disaster Recovery Payment |
|                                   |     Claims Workflow in Customer   |
|                                   |     First                         |
|                                   | -   Grant the next Relevant       |
|                                   |     Period to be paid as          |
|                                   |     identified from the Multiple  |
|                                   |     CRN on the customers Primary |
|                                   |     CRN by running the Disaster   |
|                                   |     Recovery Payment Claims       |
|                                   |     Workflow in Customer First    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If activity is for the current or |
|                                   | previous relevant period,         |
|                                   | continue with processing.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the next relevant period has a |
|                                   | future start date, place the      |
|                                   | activity on hold until the next   |
|                                   | relevant period starts.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Document the decision using the   |
|                                   | appropriate Fast Note workflow.   |
|                                   | Make sure to include claim lodged |
|                                   | on multiple CRN and previous      |
|                                   | Relevant Period paid on the       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN. The COVID-19        |
|                                   | Disaster Payment was Granted on   |
|                                   | the Primary CRN from the next     |
|                                   | Relevant Period.                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refer to the following procedures |
|                                   | to help with remediation          |
|                                   | processing:                       |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     Payment Claims                |
|                                   | -   Coding Covid-19 Disaster      |
|                                   |     Payment Claims                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm if the customer has       |
|                                   | received an incorrect rate and/or |
|                                   | overpayment on either the         |
|                                   | Multiple CRN and/or Primary CRN.  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Has the customer received an      |

Identity Remediation

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Report Suspected Fraud.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, Service Officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity Remediation, go to Step  |
|                                   | 5                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | another process:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the Identity Documents on  |
|                                   | the Multiple CRN + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Manually replicate any DOCs,  |
|                                   |     Notes and Identity            |
|                                   |     Confirmation documents onto   |
|                                   |     the primary record            |
|                                   | -   Transfer any scanned          |
|                                   |     documents lodged on the       |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN to the primary   |
|                                   |     record                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Identity Confirmation Dashboard + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Multiple CRN have a      |
|                                   | confirmed Services Australia      |
|                                   | Digital Identity Confirmation     |
|                                   | Status?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes,                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   refer to Data Quality Unit -  |
|                                   |     Identity SME for remediation. |
|                                   |     See Resources for contact     |
|                                   |     details                       |
|                                   | -   place the activity on hold    |
|                                   |     for 1 day to allow for Data   |
|                                   |     Quality Unit - Identity SME   |
|                                   |     remediation                   |
|                                   | -   upon maturity of activity     |
|                                   |     and/or digital identity       |
|                                   |     remediation on primary CRN,   |
|                                   |     go to Step 7                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No,                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   code the Services Australia   |
|                                   |     identity documents from the   |
|                                   |     multiple CRNs to the primary  |
|                                   |     record via the Identity       |
|                                   |     Dashboard in Process Direct   |
|                                   | -   see Resources for the         |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN identity         |
|                                   |     Remediation task card to view |
|                                   |     Identity documents on the     |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN, go to Step 7    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Review identity summary screens + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a          |
|                                   | confirmed Identity Confirmation   |
|                                   | on the Primary CRN?               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 1 in Table 6  |
|                                   | -   No, Enter CRN Multiple in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct (Customer      |
|                                   |     Summary) and review identity  |
|                                   |     summary screens               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If required review identity       |
|                                   | summary screens in:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Customer First                |
|                                   | -   Legacy POI                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the identity status is         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirmed, or an Interim      |
|                                   |     identity, with an alternative |
|                                   |     identity review reason code   |
|                                   |     such as Gathering Documents,  |
|                                   |     go to Step 8                  |
|                                   | -   Confirmed Transitional       |
|                                   |     contact the Identity Policy   |
|                                   |     Helpdesk by email.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Review Customer Person Details    |
|                                   | Summary (CPDS) screens + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there a name and/or date of    |
|                                   | birth mismatch between the        |
|                                   | multiple and primary CRNs?        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, refer to specific processes  |
|                                   | below and return to this file to  |
|                                   | complete the Identity Remediation |
|                                   | process                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Incorrect date of birth       |
|                                   |     recorded                      |
|                                   | -   name, go to the Process tab   |
|                                   |     of Changing the Legal name of |
|                                   |     customers or their children   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, go to Step 9                  |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Coding Identity Documents onto    |
|                                   | the Primary CRN + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Copy the required mandatory       |
|                                   | identity credential details held  |
|                                   | on Multiple CRN onto the Primary  |
|                                   | CRN.                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Staff should:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   use the Identity Summary      |
|                                   |     (Customer Identity and        |
|                                   |     Authentication) workflow in   |
|                                   |     Customer First on the         |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN to locate the    |
|                                   |     identity credentials          |
|                                   | -   code identity documents from  |
|                                   |     the Multiple CRN to the       |
|                                   |     primary record via the        |
|                                   |     Identity Dashboard in Process |
|                                   |     Direct.                       |
|                                   | -   see the Resources page for    |
|                                   |     the Multiple CRN Identity     |
|                                   |     Remediation task card for     |
|                                   |     more details                  |
|                                   | -   see Step 1 in Table 6 once    |
|                                   |     coding is completed           |

ABSTUDY (Living Allowance and/or Incidentals)

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |

| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |

|                                   | was rejected, DOC details of the  |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | was assessed or granted, go to    |
|                                   | Step 7                            |

| 7                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |

|                                   |     of address, employment income |
|                                   |     or accommodation updates      |
|                                   |     inclusive of historical       |

|                                   | screen                            |

|                                   |     Assessment Results (AR)       |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an overpayment occurs, note    |
|                                   | the debt information, including:  |

|                                   | -   types of payments (basic,     |
|                                   |     add-ons, One Off Payments)    |
|                                   | -   periods and amounts           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has a dependent   |
|                                   | child coded in care as part of    |
|                                   | the current payment, and the      |
|                                   | customer or their partner is not  |
|                                   | getting Family Tax Benefit (FTB), |
|                                   | delete care information relating  |
|                                   | to the multiple CRN in Customer   |
|                                   | First:                            |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     screen                        |

|                                   | -   FTB Shared Care (FSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   Care Alignment Details        |
|                                   |     (!CADDS) screen               |

|                                   |     activity when assessing the   |

|                                   |     Component (RAC) screen by     |

|                                   |     line                          |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: filed, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
