Age Pension

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC request. If Service        |
|                                   | Officers have the relevant skills |
|                                   | to action other work items on the |
|                                   | customer record then they should  |
|                                   | do so.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Where the request is unable to be |
|                                   | completed, for:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SSO/mySupport escalation required |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers are not          |
|                                   | re-categorise, un-assign or       |
|                                   | re-allocate the ACTDOC work item  |
|                                   | back to the pool in WLM. The      |
|                                   | ACTDOC work item will remain in   |
|                                   | the Service Officers inbox.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, only complete the relevant   |
|                                   | allocated work item.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that has been finalised   |
|                                   | on a Multiple CRN, go to Step 5   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that is In Process on a   |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, go to Step 5        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   see Step 1 in Table 5         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the claim on the Multiple  |
|                                   | CRN + Read more ...               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Multiple CRN, identify the |
|                                   | claim using the:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Assisted Customer Claim icon  |
|                                   |     on the desktop                |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First                         |
|                                   | -   Transaction icon in Process   |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identify any scanned documents    |
|                                   | used to assess this claim using:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First or                      |
|                                   | -   as part of the claim bundle   |
|                                   |     under Transaction icon in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Identify dates and                |
|                                   | circumstances + Read more ...     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Identify the start date of    |
|                                   |     the claim on the Pensions     |
|                                   |     General Information (PNGI)    |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Identify the date of receipt. |
|                                   |     This is the date the claim    |
|                                   |     was submitted or scanned      |
|                                   | -   Review the Entitlement        |
|                                   |     Delivery (RAD) screen to      |
|                                   |     determine the customer's      |
|                                   |     current payment cycle and     |
|                                   |     Entitlement Period End Date   |
|                                   |     (EPED)                        |
|                                   | -   Check for one time payments   |
|                                   |     on the One Time Payments      |
|                                   |     (OOP) screen                  |
|                                   | -   Identify any additional       |
|                                   |     change of circumstances such  |
|                                   |     as change of address,         |
|                                   |     accommodation updates         |
|                                   |     (inclusive of historical      |
|                                   |     Sharer Details Questions      |
|                                   |     (SDQ) screens), employment    |
|                                   |     income and other Income and   |
|                                   |     Asset updates provided after  |
|                                   |     the claim was submitted       |
|                                   | -   Identify any residence        |
|                                   |     information recorded on the   |
|                                   |     multiple CRN                  |
|                                   | -   Identity if a Compensation    |
|                                   |     clearance was actioned and/or |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   Identify if a Foreign Pension |
|                                   |     and/or Foreign Income and     |
|                                   |     Assets coding was recorded on |
|                                   |     the Foreign                   |
|                                   |     Income/Assets/Pensions (FIPS) |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Identify if an Complex        |
|                                   |     Assessment Officer assessment |
|                                   |     was required                  |
|                                   | -   Check for other Relationship  |
|                                   |     Links such as Authorised      |
|                                   |     Nominees, Carers, Dependent   |
|                                   |     Children on the Link Summary  |
|                                   |     (LS) screen                   |
|                                   | -   Identify if there is a        |
|                                   |     Pension Bonus Scheme          |
|                                   |     Registration or Pension Bonus |
|                                   |     claim has been lodged on      |
|                                   |     either the Primary or         |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For rejected Age Pension (AGE)    |
|                                   | claims also confirm the           |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Date of receipt. This is the  |
|                                   |     date the claim was submitted  |
|                                   |     or scanned                    |
|                                   | -   Rejection reason of the claim |
|                                   |     from the Pensions Status      |
|                                   |     History (PNSH) screen         |
|                                   | -   Date claim was rejected and   |
|                                   |     if any new information has    |
|                                   |     since been provided requiring |
|                                   |     a Reassessment                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure to capture any updates  |
|                                   | to the customer's or partner's    |
|                                   | circumstances since the claim was |
|                                   | submitted.                        |

| 16                                | Reject Age Pension on the         |
|                                   | Multiple CRN + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Consider payment delivery         |
|                                   | implications. For example, if     |
|                                   | EPED is within the next 2         |
|                                   | business days, delay any further  |
|                                   | action until customer's payment   |
|                                   | has been delivered.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reject the customer's Age Pension |
|                                   | payment on the Multiple CRN:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Benefit Action (BA)     |
|                                   | screen in Customer First or       |
|                                   | Customer Record                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: field, select |
|                                   |     AGE                           |
|                                   | -   Action: field, REJ -          |
|                                   |     Rejection                     |
|                                   | -   Reason: field, OTH - Other    |
|                                   | -   Effect Date: field,           |
|                                   |     commencement date of Age      |
|                                   |     Pension                       |
|                                   | -   Notes: field, 'Multiple       |
|                                   |     record remediation'           |
|                                   | -   Source: field, INT - Internal |
|                                   | -   Receipt Date: field, system   |
|                                   |     date                          |
|                                   | -   select Continue to go to the  |
|                                   |     Assessment Results (AR)       |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has a dependent   |
|                                   | child coded in care as part of    |
|                                   | the current payment, and the      |
|                                   | customer or their partner is not  |
|                                   | getting Family Tax Benefit (FTB), |
|                                   | delete care information relating  |
|                                   | to the multiple CRN in Customer   |
|                                   | First:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Child in Customer Care (CHC)  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   SSA Shared Care (SSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   FTB Shared Care (FSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   Care Alignment Details        |
|                                   |     (!CADDS) screen               |
|                                   | -   Child Relationships page      |
|                                   |     (!CHRE)                       |
|                                   | -   Newborn Supplement            |
|                                   |     Questionnaire (!NBSQ) screen  |
|                                   | -   Child Student/Income          |
|                                   |     Circumstances (CHSI) screen   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an overpayment occurs, DOC the |
|                                   | debt information within the       |
|                                   | activity including:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   types of payments (basic,     |
|                                   |     add-ons, One Off Payments,    |
|                                   |     etc.)                         |
|                                   | -   periods and amounts           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This information will help:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ensure the same arrears       |
|                                   |     generate in the claim         |
|                                   |     activity when assessing the   |
|                                   |     primary record, or            |
|                                   | -   debt teams in assessing debt  |
|                                   |     activities when manual        |
|                                   |     adjustments can't be          |
|                                   |     completed                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ensure a clear explanation of any |
|                                   | adjustments are recorded.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to the Rate Details (RATS) |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   select the relevant           |
|                                   |     overpayment line from the     |
|                                   |     Daily Rate Component (RAC)    |
|                                   |     table                         |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: filed, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer Record:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to the Daily Rates Summary |
|                                   |     (RATS) screen                 |
|                                   | -   go to the Customer Daily Rate |
|                                   |     Component (RAC) screen by     |
|                                   |     selecting the overpayment     |
|                                   |     line                          |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: filed, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices from the          |
|                                   | Assessment Results (AR) screen    |
|                                   | in:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer First, select the INH    |
|                                   | LTTR option in the Action table   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer Record:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to the Assessment          |
|                                   |     Consequences (ASC) screen     |
|                                   | -   in the Letter Action: field,  |
|                                   |     code 'INH'                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the rejection activity.  |

Carer Payment and/or Carer Allowance

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Where the request is unable to be |
|                                   | completed as it is:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   The Team Leader must confirm  |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and forward the       |
|                                   |     escalation email to the Data  |
|                                   |     Quality Unit                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An SSO/mySupport escalation is    |
|                                   | required                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and un-assign it         |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After actioning the Fraud         |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, only complete the relevant   |
|                                   | allocated work item.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that has been finalised   |
|                                   | on a Multiple CRN, go to Step 5   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed, go to  |
|                                   | Step 5                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the claim on the Multiple  |
|                                   | CRN + Read more ...               |

| 6                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the multiple CRN, identify |
|                                   | and take note of:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the Multiple CRN Claim ID |
|                                   | and the claim status              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The start date of the claim/s     |
|                                   | via:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Carer Payment (CP): Pensions  |
|                                   |     General Information (PNGI)    |
|                                   |     screen, and/or                |
|                                   | -   Carer Allowance (CA): Select  |
|                                   |     the care receiver via the CRS |
|                                   |     screen and then access the    |
|                                   |     Assessment history (CJAA)     |
|                                   |     screen.                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The date of receipt. This is the  |
|                                   | date the claim was submitted or   |
|                                   | scanned                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Relationship Links as such        |
|                                   | Authorised Nominee's, Dependent   |
|                                   | Children                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Care Receiver details from Care   |
|                                   | Receiver Summary Screen (CRS)     |
|                                   | screen:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Name                          |
|                                   | -   CRN                           |
|                                   | -   Care Type (CP/CAR and/or      |
|                                   |     CDA/CA)                       |
|                                   | -   Adult/Child status            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the date paid + 1 date on |
|                                   | the Payment Summary (PS) screen   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm if a Complex Assessment   |
|                                   | Office (CAO) determination was    |
|                                   | actioned and/or required          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm if a Compensation         |
|                                   | clearance was actioned and/or     |
|                                   | required                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Entitlement Delivery (RAD)    |
|                                   | screen to determine the           |
|                                   | customer's current payment cycle  |
|                                   | and Entitlement Period End Date   |
|                                   | (EPED)                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | One time payments on the One Time |
|                                   | Payments (OTPSUM or OOP) screens, |
|                                   | for example Economic Support      |
|                                   | Payments                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review any relevant additional    |
|                                   | change of circumstances such as   |
|                                   | change of address, employment     |
|                                   | income or accommodation updates   |
|                                   | inclusive of historical Sharer    |
|                                   | Details Questions (SDQ) screen    |
|                                   | updates                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For rejected Carers claims also   |
|                                   | confirm the following:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the date of receipt. This |
|                                   | is the date the claim was         |
|                                   | submitted or scanned              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the rejection reason via: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Carer Payment (CA): Pensions  |
|                                   |     Status History (PNSH) screen, |
|                                   |     and/or                        |
|                                   | -   Carer Allowance (CA): Select  |
|                                   |     the care receiver via the CRS |
|                                   |     screen and then access the    |
|                                   |     Assessment history (CJAA)     |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm the date the claim was    |
|                                   | rejected/finalised and if any new |
|                                   | evidence has since been provided  |
|                                   | for a Reassessment                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure to capture any updates  |
|                                   | to the customer's circumstances   |
|                                   | since the claim was submitted.    |

|                                   | provided in the original claim,   |
|                                   | and any other change of           |
|                                   | circumstances identified at Step  |
|                                   | 6, including:                     |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Treating Health Professional  |
|                                   |     (THP) report: Adult medical   |
|                                   |     details (ADMD) screen         |
|                                   | -   Care Needs Assessment (CNA):  |
|                                   |     Care receiver task selector   |
|                                   |     (CETS)                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | the EPED on the RAD screen to     |
|                                   | align with the customer's current |
|                                   | payment cycle                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Code any identified change of     |
|                                   | circumstances updates advised     |
|                                   | since the rejection that may      |
|                                   | affect original claim outcome     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Code any additional change of     |
|                                   | circumstances updates such as     |
|                                   | Change of Address, Employment     |
|                                   | Income, Accommodation Summary     |
|                                   | updates (inclusive of historical  |
|                                   | Sharer Details Questions (SDQ)    |
|                                   | screen - CP only)                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has not met       |
|                                   | Identity Confirmation within the  |
|                                   | Identity Confirmation Dashboard,  |
|                                   | ensure Alternative Identification |
|                                   | is recorded on the Proof of       |
|                                   | Identity (POI) screen, reflecting |
|                                   | Reason for Insufficient POI with  |
|                                   | Gathering Documents (GD)          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the claim activity       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ensure the grant/rejection DOC    |

|                                   |     claim                         |

|                                   | -   the Claim ID                  |
|                                   | -   if a Secretary initiated      |
|                                   |     review of decision was        |
|                                   |     implemented                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices (do not inhibit   |
|                                   | advices where a Secretary         |
|                                   | initiated review of decision was  |
|                                   | implemented):                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   From the AR screen, go to ASC |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   In Letter Action: field, code |
|                                   |     'INH'                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If Alternative Identity was       |
|                                   | recorded within claim             |
|                                   | remediation, please refer to      |
|                                   | Alternative Identity status in    |
|                                   | Identity Confirmation Dashboard   |
|                                   | remaining Open after claim        |
|                                   | finalised to ensure Identity      |
|                                   | Confirmation Dashboard action is  |
|                                   | completed. The Resources page     |
|                                   | contains a link to this item.     |
|                                   |                                   |

Concession Cards

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Where the request is unable to be |
|                                   | completed as it is:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   The Team Leader must confirm  |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and forward the       |
|                                   |     escalation email to the Data  |
|                                   |     Quality Unit                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An SSO/mySupport escalation is    |
|                                   | required                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After actioning the Fraud         |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, only complete the relevant   |
|                                   | allocated work item.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that has been finalised   |
|                                   | on a multiple CRN, go to Step 5   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed, go to  |
|                                   | Step 5                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   see Step 1 in Table 5         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the claim or renewal on    |
|                                   | the multiple CRN + Read more ...  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the multiple CRN, identify the |
|                                   | claim or renewal the customer is  |
|                                   | currently receiving using the:    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Assisted Customer Claim icon  |
|                                   |     on the desktop or             |
|                                   | -   Transaction icon in Process   |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identify any scanned documents    |
|                                   | used to assess this claim or      |
|                                   | renewal using:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First or                      |
|                                   | -   as part of the claim bundle   |
|                                   |     under Transaction icon in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the multiple CRN, identify |
|                                   | and take note of:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the Multiple CRN      |
|                                   |     Claim ID and the claim status |
|                                   | -   The concession start date of  |
|                                   |     the card on the Concession    |
|                                   |     Entitlement Summary (CCIS)    |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   The date of receipt. This is  |
|                                   |     the date the claim was        |
|                                   |     submitted or scanned          |
|                                   | -   Relationship Links as such    |
|                                   |     Authorised Nominee's, Carers, |
|                                   |     Dependents, including         |
|                                   |     Children                      |
|                                   | -   Concession dependant details  |
|                                   |     on Concession Dependant       |
|                                   |     Summary (MCDS) screen         |
|                                   | -   One time payments on the One  |
|                                   |     Time Payments (OTPSUM or OOP) |
|                                   |     screens, for example Economic |
|                                   |     Support Payments              |
|                                   | -   Review any relevant           |
|                                   |     additional change of          |
|                                   |     circumstances such as change  |
|                                   |     of address, employment income |
|                                   | -   Confirm if a Compensation     |
|                                   |     clearance was actioned and/or |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   For Low Income Health Care    |
|                                   |     Card (LIC), confirm if a      |
|                                   |     Complex Assessment Office     |
|                                   |     (CAO) determination was       |
|                                   |     actioned and/or required      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For rejected card claims and      |
|                                   | renewals also confirm the         |
|                                   | following:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the date of receipt.  |
|                                   |     This is the date the claim or |
|                                   |     renewal was submitted or      |
|                                   |     scanned                       |
|                                   | -   Confirm the rejection reason  |
|                                   |     of the card on the Service    |
|                                   |     Reason Summary (SRS) screen   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the date of claim or  |
|                                   |     renewal was                   |
|                                   |     rejected/finalised and if any |
|                                   |     new evidence has since been   |
|                                   |     provided for a Reassessment   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure to capture any updates  |
|                                   | to the customer's circumstances   |
|                                   | since the claim was submitted.    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Transfer information + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Manually replicate any DOCs,  |
|                                   |     Notes and Identity            |
|                                   |     Confirmation documents        |
|                                   |     relevant to the claim onto    |
|                                   |     the primary CRN               |
|                                   | -   Transfer any scanned          |
|                                   |     documents lodged on the       |
|                                   |     multiple CRN since the        |
|                                   |     original claim to the primary |
|                                   |     CRN                           |
|                                   | -   Code identity documents from  |
|                                   |     the multiple CRN to the       |
|                                   |     primary CRN via the Identity  |
|                                   |     Dashboard in Process Direct.  |
|                                   |     For further details, see the  |
|                                   |     Resources page for the        |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN Identity         |
|                                   |     Remediation task card         |
|                                   | -   Print and scan Multiple CRN   |
|                                   |     claim onto Primary CRN (If    |
|                                   |     claim is a paper claim -      |
|                                   |     transfer claim as part of     |
|                                   |     Transfer any scanned          |

|                                   |     print the Claim Summary.      |
|                                   |     Print and scan Multiple CRN   |
|                                   |     claim onto Primary CRN        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See the Resources page for the    |
|                                   | Multiple CRN Identity Remediation |
|                                   | task card for further details.    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Identity Confirmation Status +    |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the primary CRN have a       |
|                                   | confirmed Services Australia and  |
