+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Disability Support Pension (DSP)

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the request |
|                                   | as it is:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   The Team Leader must confirm  |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and forward the       |
|                                   |     escalation email to the Data  |
|                                   |     Quality Unit                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | An SSO/mySupport escalation is    |
|                                   | required                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, only complete the relevant   |
|                                   | allocated work item.              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Table 6                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that has been finalised   |
|                                   | on a Multiple CRN, go to Step 5   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a claim that is In Process on a   |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, go to Step 5        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Table 4         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Locate the claim on the multiple  |
|                                   | CRN + Read more ...               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the Multiple CRN, identify the |
|                                   | claim the customer is currently   |
|                                   | receiving payment for using the:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Search Online Claims in       |
|                                   |     Customer First                |
|                                   | -   Assisted Customer Claim icon  |
|                                   |     on the desktop or             |
|                                   | -   Transaction icon in Process   |
|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identify any scanned documents    |
|                                   | used to assess this claim using:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First or                      |
|                                   | -   as part of the claim bundle   |
|                                   |     under Transaction icon in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim has been finalised:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the start date of the |
|                                   |     claim on the Pension Status   |
|                                   |     History (PNSH) screen         |
|                                   | -   Confirm the date of receipt.  |
|                                   |     This is the date the claim    |
|                                   |     was submitted or scanned      |
|                                   | -   Review the Entitlement        |
|                                   |     Delivery (RAD) screen to      |
|                                   |     determine the customer's      |
|                                   |     current payment cycle and     |
|                                   |     Entitlement Period End Date   |
|                                   |     (EPED)                        |
|                                   | -   One time payments on the One  |
|                                   |     Time Payments (OOP) screen    |
|                                   | -   Review any relevant           |
|                                   |     additional change of          |
|                                   |     circumstances such as change  |
|                                   |     of address, employment income |
|                                   |     or accommodation updates      |
|                                   |     inclusive of historical       |
|                                   |     Sharer Details Questions      |
|                                   |     (SDQ) screen updates          |
|                                   | -   Confirm rate of payment.      |
|                                   |     Consider age, independence    |
|                                   |     status and payability. Refer  |
|                                   |     to Pensions Disability        |
|                                   |     Information (PDI) screen and  |
|                                   |     Payment Summary (PS) screen   |
|                                   | -   Confirm Jobseeker             |
|                                   |     Identification Number         |
|                                   | -   Confirm if a Complex          |
|                                   |     Assessment Office (CAO)       |
|                                   |     determination was required    |
|                                   | -   Confirm if a Compensation     |
|                                   |     Clearance was required        |
|                                   | -   Confirm Nominee Arrangements  |
|                                   | -   Identify any residence        |
|                                   |     information recorded on the   |
|                                   |     multiple CRN                  |
|                                   | -   Confirm if outcome based on   |
|                                   |     Medical Assessment Team (MAT) |
|                                   |     recommendation, Job Capacity  |
|                                   |     Assessment or Disability      |
|                                   |     Medical Assessment            |
|                                   | -   Confirm any deductions such   |
|                                   |     as Centrepay, tax deductions, |
|                                   |     child support payments        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For rejected Disability Support   |
|                                   | Pension (DSP) claims also confirm |
|                                   | the following:                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the date of receipt.  |
|                                   |     This is the date the claim    |
|                                   |     was submitted or scanned      |
|                                   | -   Confirm the rejection reason  |
|                                   |     of the claim on the Pensions  |
|                                   |     Status History (PNSH) screens |
|                                   | -   Confirm the date of claim was |
|                                   |     rejected / finalised          |
|                                   | -   Confirm Jobseeker             |
|                                   |     Identification Number (JSID)  |
|                                   |     Program of Support            |
|                                   |     participation requirements    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make sure to capture any updates  |
|                                   | to the customer's circumstances   |
|                                   | since the claim was submitted.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If DSP claim is still in          |
|                                   | progress:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Confirm date of receipt. This |
|                                   |     is the date the claim was     |
|                                   |     submitted or scanned.         |
|                                   | -   Review DSP NCL Progress Doc   |
|                                   |     to establish where claim has  |
|                                   |     progressed to                 |

| 16                                | Reject the income support payment |
|                                   | on the Multiple CRN + Read more   |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Consider payment delivery         |
|                                   | implications. For example, if     |
|                                   | EPED is within the next 2         |
|                                   | business days, delay any further  |
|                                   | action until customer's payment   |
|                                   | has been delivered.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Reject the customer's income      |
|                                   | support payment on the Multiple   |
|                                   | CRN:                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Benefit Action (BA)     |
|                                   | screen in Customer First or       |
|                                   | Customer Record                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Service Reason: field, select |
|                                   |     the relevant payment type     |
|                                   | -   Action: field, REJ -          |
|                                   |     Rejection                     |
|                                   | -   Reason: field, OTH - Other    |
|                                   | -   Effect Date: field,           |
|                                   |     commencement date of the      |
|                                   |     current payment               |
|                                   | -   Notes: field, 'Multiple       |
|                                   |     record remediation'           |
|                                   | -   Source: field, INT - Internal |
|                                   | -   Receipt Date: field, system   |
|                                   |     date                          |
|                                   | -   select Continue to go to the  |
|                                   |     Assessment Results (AR)       |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer has a dependent   |
|                                   | child coded in care as part of    |
|                                   | the current payment, and the      |
|                                   | customer or their partner, is not |
|                                   | in receipt of Family Tax Benefit  |
|                                   | (FTB), delete care information    |
|                                   | relating to the dependent child   |
|                                   | on the multiple CRN in Customer   |
|                                   | First:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Child in Customer Care (CHC)  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   SSA Shared Care (SSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   FTB Shared Care (FSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   Care Alignment Details        |
|                                   |     (!CADDS) screen               |
|                                   | -   Child Relationships page      |
|                                   |     (!CHRE)                       |
|                                   | -   Newborn Supplement            |
|                                   |     Questionnaire (!NBSQ) screen  |
|                                   | -   Child Student/Income          |
|                                   |     Circumstances (CHSI) screen   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an overpayment occurs note the |
|                                   | debt information, including:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   types of payments (basic,     |
|                                   |     add-ons, One Off Payments)    |
|                                   | -   periods and amounts           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This information will help:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ensure the same arrears are   |
|                                   |     generated in the claim        |
|                                   |     activity when assessing on    |
|                                   |     the primary record, or        |
|                                   | -   debt teams assess debt shells |
|                                   |     when manual adjustments       |
|                                   |     cannot be made                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ensure a clear explanation of any |
|                                   | adjustments are recorded.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Rate Details (RATS) |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     overpayment line from the     |
|                                   |     Daily Rate Component (RAC)    |
|                                   |     table                         |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: field, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer Record:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Daily Rates Summary |
|                                   |     (RATS) screen                 |
|                                   | -   Go to the Customer Daily Rate |
|                                   |     Component (RAC) screen by     |
|                                   |     selecting the overpayment     |
|                                   |     line                          |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: field, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices from the          |
|                                   | Assessment Results (AR) screen    |
|                                   | in:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer First, select the INH    |
|                                   | LTTR option in the Action table   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer Record:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to the Assessment          |
|                                   |     Consequences (ASC) screen     |
|                                   | -   in the Letter Action: field,  |
|                                   |     code 'INH'                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The cancellation will result in a |
|                                   | REJection outcome on the AR and   |
|                                   | PNSH screens.                     |

Families

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Send an email to the Team Leader. |
|                                   | Record the Work Item ID and Work  |
|                                   | Item Type in the email subject    |
|                                   | line. In the body of the email,   |
|                                   | record the DQU requested action   |
|                                   | and why the request is out of     |
|                                   | scope                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The Team Leader must confirm that |
|                                   | the request is out of scope of    |
|                                   | their Service Officer and forward |
|                                   | the escalation email to the Data  |
|                                   | Quality Unit                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The following remediation         |
|                                   | activities are out of scope and   |
|                                   | should be referred back to DQU:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   FTB crossing financial years  |
|                                   | -   All Paid Parental Leave       |
|                                   |     activities                    |
|                                   | -   Child Care Benefit (CCB) and  |
|                                   |     Child Care Subsidy (CCS)      |
|                                   |     activities where attendance   |
|                                   |     has been recorded on the      |
|                                   |     multiple CRN                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | SSO/mySupport escalation required |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occur when  |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, Service officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Table 6                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a Multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed, go to  |
|                                   | Step 5                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a Multiple CRN where FTB claim    |
|                                   | has been paid or is FTB/CUR, go   |
|                                   | to Step 6                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a Multiple CRN where DAP has been |
|                                   | paid, go to Step 7                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a multiple child CRN where the    |
|                                   | customer has been paid FTB or     |
|                                   | DAP, go to Step 8                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a multiple / intertwined record   |
|                                   | where the customer has received   |
|                                   | CCS, go to Step 9                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Table 4         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |

| 5                                 | A Multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review the Multiple CRN, and      |

|                                   | claim lodged.                     |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For paper claims, cancel the      |
|                                   | claim on Activity List (AL)       |

|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     and notes relevant to the     |
|                                   |     claim onto the primary record |
|                                   | -   Transfer any scanned          |
|                                   |     documents lodged on the       |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN since the        |
|                                   |     original claim to the primary |
|                                   |     record                        |
|                                   | -   Print and Scan Multiple CRN   |
|                                   |     claim onto Primary CRN        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For online claims, cancel the     |
|                                   | started claim on AL on the        |
|                                   | multiple CRN                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Mark the claim lodged on the      |
|                                   | multiple CRN as:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   'not required' for            |
|                                   |     FTB/PPL/DAP or                |
|                                   | -   'withdrawn' for CCS           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Transfer information:             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Manually replicate any DOCs   |
|                                   |     and notes relevant to the     |
|                                   |     claim onto the primary record |
|                                   | -   Transfer any scanned          |
|                                   |     documents lodged on the       |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN since the        |
|                                   |     original claim to the primary |
|                                   |     record                        |
|                                   | -   Print and scan Multiple CRN   |
|                                   |     claim onto Primary CRN        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the primary record:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Re-index the claim. CCS       |
|                                   |     claims cannot be re-indexed.  |
|                                   |     Re-enter the details of the   |
|                                   |     claim on the primary CRN via  |
|                                   |     the ACC. See Cancelling claim |
|                                   |     activities and re-indexing    |
|                                   |     claims                        |
|                                   | -   Record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   Complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a Job      |
|                                   | Seeker Identification (JSID)      |
|                                   | number on the Multiple CRN?       |

|                                   | -   No, see Table 5               |

| 6                                 | A Multiple CRN where FTB has been |
|                                   | paid or is FTB/CUR + Read more    |
|                                   | ...                               |

|                                   |     Take note of the AMR          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Multiple CRN:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Delete care information in the    |
|                                   | following order:                  |

|                                   |     care 'NCC' on the Child in    |

|                                   |     into care                     |

|                                   | data is sent to primary CRN claim |
|                                   | activity                          |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     claim onto Primary CRN        |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     paid                          |

|                                   | -   Record details on a DOC       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a Job      |
|                                   | Seeker Identification (JSID)      |
|                                   | number on the Multiple CRN?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, see Table 2              |
|                                   | -   No, see Table 5               |

Students

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occurs when |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim and              |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN, Service Officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a draft claim or a claim that has |
|                                   | been finalised on a Multiple CRN, |
|                                   | go to Step 5                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a Multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed, go to  |
|                                   | Step 5                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking to a partner with a       |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, see Step 1 in Table |
|                                   | 4                                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |

|                                   | was assessed or granted, go to    |

|                                   | (FTB) delete care information     |
|                                   | relating to the dependent child   |
|                                   | on the multiple CRN in Customer   |
|                                   | First:                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Child in Customer Care (CHC)  |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   SSA Shared Care (SSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   FTB Shared Care (FSC) screen  |
|                                   | -   Care Alignment Details        |
|                                   |     (!CADDS) screen               |
|                                   | -   Child Relationships page      |
|                                   |     (!CHRE)                       |
|                                   | -   Newborn Supplement            |
|                                   |     Questionnaire (!NBSQ) screen  |
|                                   | -   Child Student/Income          |
|                                   |     Circumstances (CHSI) screen   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an overpayment occurs note the |
|                                   | debt information, including:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   types of payments (basic,     |
|                                   |     add-ons, One Off Payments)    |
|                                   | -   periods and amounts           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This information will help:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   ensure the same arrears are   |
|                                   |     generated in the claim        |
|                                   |     activity when assessing the   |
|                                   |     primary record, or            |
|                                   | -   debt teams assess debt shells |
|                                   |     when manual adjustments       |
|                                   |     cannot be made                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ensure a clear explanation of any |
|                                   | adjustments are recorded.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer First:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Rate Details (RATS) |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   Select the relevant           |
|                                   |     overpayment line from the     |
|                                   |     Daily Rate Component (RAC)    |
|                                   |     table                         |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: filed, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer Record:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the Daily Rates Summary |
|                                   |     (RATS) screen                 |
|                                   | -   Go to the Customer Daily Rate |
|                                   |     Component (RAC) screen by     |
|                                   |     selecting the overpayment     |
|                                   |     line                          |
|                                   | -   Man Adj $: filed, code $0 in  |
|                                   |     all lines                     |
|                                   | -   Man Adj Rsn: ADJ - adjustment |
|                                   | -   Repeat for all lines of       |
|                                   |     overpayment on the RAC screen |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices from the          |
|                                   | Assessment Results (AR) screen    |
|                                   | in:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer First, select the INH    |
|                                   | LTTR option in the Action table   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Customer Record:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   go to the Assessment          |
|                                   |     Consequences (ASC) screen     |
|                                   | -   in the Letter Action: field,  |
|                                   |     code 'INH'                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer is receiving      |
|                                   | Youth Allowance as a dependent?   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 13            |
|                                   | -   No, finalise the cancelation  |
|                                   |     activity and DOC the record   |
|                                   |     Note: the cancellation will   |
|                                   |     result in a REJection outcome |
|                                   |     on the AR and ABH screens     |

|                                   | relevant Current PIT parent. If   |
|                                   | the PIT Link Start Date is:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | prior to the most recent YA Start |
|                                   | Date, end date the PIT link:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   End Date: field, the day      |
|                                   |     prior to the current YA Start |
|                                   |     Date                          |
|                                   | -   End Reason: field, NLR - No   |
|                                   |     longer required               |
|                                   | -   Action: field, C - Correct    |
|                                   | -   Enter                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | on, or after, the most recent YA  |
|                                   | Start Date, delete the PIT link:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Action: field, D - Delete     |
|                                   | -   Enter                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Repeat the steps for each Current |
|                                   | PIT parent, and then Finalise the |

|                                   |     exist on the Reference Number |
|                                   |     (NU) screen on the Multiple   |
|                                   |     CRN                           |
|                                   | -   Customer CRN: field, record   |
|                                   |     the Primary CRN               |
|                                   | -   Date of Receipt: field,       |
|                                   |     record the date of claim      |
|                                   |     lodgement from Step 7         |
|                                   | -   select Create Claim           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Review both Multiple CRN and      |
|                                   | Primary CRN to determine if new   |
|                                   | information has been provided     |
|                                   | since the rejection that may      |
|                                   | result in either a Reassessment   |
|                                   | of the Original Decision made on  |
|                                   | the Multiple CRN.                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Code all relevant information     |
|                                   | provided in the original claim,   |
|                                   | and any other change of           |
|                                   | circumstances identified at Step  |
|                                   | 7, including:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   the Start Date on the Date of |
|                                   |     Commencement (NDC) screen     |
|                                   | -   the EPED on the RAD screen to |
|                                   |     align with the customer's     |
|                                   |     current payment cycle         |
|                                   | -   Code any additional change of |
|                                   |     circumstances updates such as |
|                                   |     Change of Address, Employment |
|                                   |     Income, Accommodation Summary |
|                                   |     updates (inclusive of         |
|                                   |     historical Sharer Details     |
|                                   |     Questions (SDQ) screen        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete a Secretary initiated    |
|                                   | review of decision if an error in |
|                                   | the original decision is          |
|                                   | identified, evidence suggests the |
|                                   | decision was incorrect or the     |
|                                   | interpretation of the legislation |
|                                   | has changed                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer was current on an |
|                                   | income support payment on the     |
|                                   | Multiple CRN, on the AR screen:   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices from the          |
|                                   | Assessment Consequences (ASC)     |
|                                   | screen (do not inhibit advices    |
|                                   | where a Secretary initiated       |
|                                   | review of decision was            |
|                                   | implemented) and Letter Action:   |
|                                   | field, code 'INH'                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manually adjust any arrears, to   |
|                                   | offset against any overpayments   |
|                                   | manually adjusted at Step 9:      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   from the ELD screen           |
|                                   | -   enter RAC in the Super Key    |
|                                   |     field                         |
|                                   | -   locate arrears period/s       |
|                                   | -   code Manual Adjustment: 0     |
|                                   | -   code Manual Adjustment        |
|                                   |     reason: ADJ - adjustment      |
|                                   | -   select Update                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manually adjust any duplicate     |
|                                   | payments of the Economic Support  |
|                                   | Payment and Coronavirus           |
|                                   | Supplement payment, to offset     |
|                                   | against any overpayments manually |
|                                   | adjusted at Step 9:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   from the ELD screen           |
|                                   | -   go to the OOP screen          |
|                                   | -   zero any duplicate Economic   |
|                                   |     Support Payment and           |
|                                   |     Coronavirus Supplement        |
|                                   |     payments                      |
|                                   | -   enter reason code MCR -       |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manual adjustment of arrears on   |
|                                   | RAC will only be available if the |
|                                   | customer is profiled as a         |
|                                   | notification reporter.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the customer recorded as a     |
|                                   | statement reporter (i.e. 2we on   |
|                                   | RPRS)?                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 20                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, finalise the claim activity:  |

|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Source: INT - Internal            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Date of Receipt: Date activity is |
|                                   | created                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Notes: record information         |
|                                   | detailing potential overpayment.  |

|                                   | the Secretary initiated review of |
|                                   | decision correct the customer's   |

|                                   | -   Position                      |
|                                   | -   Transfer to Region            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select Continue                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The review has now been set and   |
|                                   | will appear on the customer's     |
|                                   | Future Activity List (FAL) screen |
|                                   | with the status of REV            |
