Tertiary Access Payment (TAP)

Table 1

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | DQU ACTDOC has been sent for      |
|                                   | action + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU ACTDOC work items are         |
|                                   | directed to Service Officers who  |
|                                   | carry active skill tag            |
|                                   | capabilities to complete the      |
|                                   | request.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The DQU work item will present as |
|                                   | either:                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Multiple CRN        |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REQ_DQU) or |
|                                   | -   DQU SDN - Intertwined CRN     |
|                                   |     Remediation (ZIAM_REM_DQU)    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A record may have several DQU     |
|                                   | work items. Action the work item  |
|                                   | allocated. The Work item ID       |
|                                   | corresponds with the AMR of the   |
|                                   | request. If Service Officers have |
|                                   | the relevant skills to action     |
|                                   | other work items on the customer  |
|                                   | record then they should do so.    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | DQU work items have a high        |
|                                   | priority, wherever possible       |
|                                   | complete on day 0. Annotate the   |
|                                   | ACTDOC if delays occur.           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the Service Officer have the |
|                                   | capability to complete the        |
|                                   | request?                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 2              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Escalate DQU work items + Read    |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If unable to complete the         |
|                                   | request:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Out of scope                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the Team     |
|                                   |     Leader. Record the Work Item  |
|                                   |     ID and Work Item Type in the  |
|                                   |     email subject line. In the    |
|                                   |     body of the email, record the |
|                                   |     DQU requested action and why  |
|                                   |     the request is out of scope   |
|                                   | -   Team Leaders must confirm     |
|                                   |     that the request is out of    |
|                                   |     scope of their Service        |
|                                   |     Officer and reallocate work   |
|                                   |     item to the pool              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Support escalation required       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Escalate according to Service |
|                                   |     Officer's divisional process  |
|                                   | -   Send an email to the          |
|                                   |     Multiples Helpdesk. Record    |
|                                   |     the Work Item ID and Work     |
|                                   |     Item Type in the email        |
|                                   |     subject line. In the body of  |
|                                   |     the email, record the DQU     |
|                                   |     requested action and why the  |
|                                   |     request is escalated          |
|                                   | -   Do not re-categorise,         |
|                                   |     un-assign or re-allocate the  |
|                                   |     ACTDOC work item back to the  |
|                                   |     pool in WLM. The ACTDOC work  |
|                                   |     item will remain in the       |
|                                   |     Service Officers inbox. DQU   |
|                                   |     will review the ACTDOC work   |
|                                   |     item and unassign it          |
|                                   |     following the review          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Procedure ends here.              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Report Identity Fraud + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identity fraud and attempts to    |
|                                   | commit identity fraud occurs when |
|                                   | a person uses an identity other   |
|                                   | than their own legal name to:     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   create a CRN                  |
|                                   | -   make a claim, and             |
|                                   | -   receive a payment they are    |
|                                   |     not entitled to receive       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To prevent Identity fraud, check  |
|                                   | for indicators that may show a    |
|                                   | deliberate attempt to commit      |
|                                   | fraud, such as:                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Different payment             |
|                                   |     destinations provided         |
|                                   | -   Different mobile phone        |
|                                   |     numbers provided              |
|                                   | -   Not declaring a previous      |
|                                   |     name/s                        |
|                                   | -   Multiple myGov accounts for   |
|                                   |     the initial linking of        |
|                                   |     records and ongoing           |
|                                   |     transactions                  |
|                                   | -   Making a second claim when    |
|                                   |     already on a benefit          |
|                                   | -   Identity documents lodged     |
|                                   |     with similar and recent issue |
|                                   |     dates                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If a staff member identifies      |
|                                   | fraud, they must Report Suspected |
|                                   | Fraud.                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is no identified fraud   |
|                                   | or after actioning the Fraud      |
|                                   | referral, go to Step 4.           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Work item + Read more ...         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Do not return work items to DQU.  |
|                                   | There may be more than 1 ACTDOC   |
|                                   | work item from DQU on a single    |
|                                   | CRN. Service Officers should only |
|                                   | complete the work items if they   |
|                                   | have the capability to do so.     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an ACTDOC work item is         |
|                                   | accidentally closed without       |
|                                   | completing the action, contact    |
|                                   | DQU immediately. The Resources    |
|                                   | page has a link to their contact  |
|                                   | details.                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine if the work item        |
|                                   | relates to:                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | linking the customer's myGov      |
|                                   | account to a Primary CRN, and     |
|                                   | this is the only action required, |
|                                   | see Step 1 in Table 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a draft claim or a claim that has |
|                                   | been finalised on a Multiple CRN, |
|                                   | go to Step 5                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | a Multiple CRN with a claim that  |
|                                   | has not yet been assessed, go to  |
|                                   | Step 5                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | to another process:               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   action the request            |
|                                   | -   record details on a DOC       |
|                                   | -   complete the ACTDOC work item |
|                                   | -   procedure ends here           |

|                                   |     on the desktop or             |

|                                   |     Direct                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Identify any scanned documents    |
|                                   | used to assess this claim using:  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Document Tools in Customer    |
|                                   |     First or                      |
|                                   | -   as part of the claim bundle   |
|                                   |     under Transaction icon in     |
|                                   |     Process Direct                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the claim:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | is in draft, contact the customer |
|                                   | to:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   advise them that they will be |
|                                   |     required to commence/submit a |
|                                   |     new claim on the Primary CRN  |
|                                   | -   link the customer's myGov     |
|                                   |     account to the Primary CRN,   |
|                                   |     see Step 1 in Table 5         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | was rejected, DOC details of the  |
|                                   | outcome on the Primary CRN.       |
|                                   | Procedure ends here               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | granted, go to Step 6             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | is in process, go to Step 6       |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Confirm dates and circumstances + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |

Jobseeker registration on multiple record

Table 2

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Check the JSID number + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Compare the JSID number on the    |
|                                   | multiple record to the primary    |
|                                   | record.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a multiple |
|                                   | CRN and Multiple JSID?            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, go to Step 3              |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Customer has multiple CRN and     |
|                                   | JSID + Read more ...              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirmation of Primary JSID is   |
|                                   | required with the Department of   |
|                                   | Education, Skills and Employment. |
|                                   | To confirm, raise a Digital       |
|                                   | Assistant Roxy ICT ticket.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | From the Customer Summary tile in |
|                                   | Process Direct, open Roxy, select |
|                                   | Raise Incident and complete the   |
|                                   | following fields:                 |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Pre-requisites                |
|                                   | -   Operational Blueprint         |
|                                   |     consulted                     |
|                                   | -   NNU Consulted                 |
|                                   | -   Been granted a bypass         |
|                                   | -   Bypass Reason - JSID Multiple |
|                                   | -   Related Benefit - Employer    |
|                                   |     Requested Review              |
|                                   | -   Known Issue - JSID Multiple   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the Issue description field,   |
|                                   | located in the Incident Details   |
|                                   | section record the following      |
|                                   | information:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Name:                         |
|                                   | -   DOB:                          |
|                                   | -   Gender:                       |
|                                   | -   Multiple CRN:                 |
|                                   | -   Primary CRN:                  |
|                                   | -   Multiple JSID/XRN:            |
|                                   | -   Primary JSID/XRN:             |
|                                   | -   Income Support Payment:       |
|                                   |     Record applicable payment -   |
|                                   |     JSP/YAL/DSP/PP                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Submit Roxy Incident              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Table 5.                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Customer has a Multiple CRN and   |
|                                   | Single JSID + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does customer have an Employment  |
|                                   | Services Assessment (ESAt)?       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, Employment Services          |
|                                   | Assessment is submitted           |
|                                   |                                   |

|                                   |     Transformation team advising  |
|                                   |     outstanding ESAt on           |
|                                   |     customer's JSID number and    |
|                                   |     Multiple CRN number           |
|                                   | -   See Table 5                   |

|                                   | Assessment is finalised, go to    |

|                                   | Unlink the JSID:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Client Department       |
|                                   | interactions (CD) screen          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Access to the CD screen is    |
|                                   |     restricted                    |
|                                   | -   Request access via ICT        |
|                                   |     Security Portal. The CDIA -   |
|                                   |     CLIENT DEPARTMENT             |
|                                   |     INTERACTIONS resource is      |
|                                   |     required. It is located       |
|                                   |     within the Income Security    |
|                                   |     Category for Mainframe        |
|                                   |     Applications                  |

|                                   | System                            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Key 'UNL' in Action               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter the reason for unlinking,   |
|                                   | (indicate corrective action       |
|                                   | required to link JSID to correct  |
|                                   | Primary CRN)                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Enter Source                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Press Enter                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | A warning message will display,   |
|                                   | key 'Y' and press Enter to        |
|                                   | confirm the unlinking             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refer to the Operations Design    |
|                                   | and Transformation team if:       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a data validation error is    |
|                                   |     received and                  |
|                                   | -   the unlink is not performed   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | This can occur when Department of |
|                                   | Education, Skills and Employment  |
|                                   | holds a different link on their   |
|                                   | side.                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The unlinking process may take    |
|                                   | overnight to complete.            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | JSID linking + Read more ...      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To link the Primary CRN to the    |
|                                   | Single JSID:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Open Customer First with      |
|                                   |     Primary CRN                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Looking for Work   |
|                                   |     workflow via Quick Links menu |
|                                   |     or using search               |
|                                   | -   A list of matching customers  |
|                                   |     with Department of Education, |
|                                   |     Skills and Employment will    |
|                                   |     show                          |
|                                   | -   Select the correct Customer   |
|                                   |     Name hyperlink to the correct |
|                                   |     JSID                          |
|                                   | -   Select the Continue button    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Note:                             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the record does not match  |
|                                   |     the JSID, press Back to       |
|                                   |     select another JSID from the  |
|                                   |     list                          |
|                                   | -   If E020C3 - XID already       |
|                                   |     linked to CRN: error presents |
|                                   |     in the top right hand corner  |
|                                   |     of the External Personal      |
|                                   |     Details (XPED) screen, this   |
|                                   |     will indicate that the        |
|                                   |     unlinking process has not     |
|                                   |     been actioned correctly with  |
|                                   |     either Agency records via the |
|                                   |     CD screen or Department of    |
|                                   |     Education, Skills and         |
|                                   |     Employment. This can take an  |
|                                   |     overnight action to unlink    |
|                                   |     from the Multiple CRN         |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 6                                 | Confirm the JSID Link + Read more |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | After confirming the JSID link,   |
|                                   | the Looking For Work question set |
|                                   | will show. This is not required   |
|                                   | if only linking the JSID. Select  |
|                                   | the Cancel workflow option to     |
|                                   | quit the workflow.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the Jobseeker activity:        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | cancels/completes, go to Step 7   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | does not cancel/complete, refer   |
|                                   | the case to Operations Design and |
|                                   | Transformation team. For staff    |
|                                   | in:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Operations Design and         |
|                                   |     Transformation team, see      |
|                                   |     Table 3                       |
|                                   | -   All other teams, see Table 5  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Confirm that the multiple CRN     |
|                                   | does not present with a JSR/ACT   |
|                                   | status on the Benefit Status      |
|                                   | Line. If there is a JSR/ACT       |
|                                   | recorded, refer the case to       |
|                                   | Operations Design and             |
|                                   | Transformations Team.             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Primary CRN - Employment Services |
|                                   | Assessment (ESAt) Referral + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Does the customer have a          |
|                                   | finalised Employment Services     |
|                                   | Assessment?                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, refer Primary CRN for an     |
|                                   | Employment Services Assessment.   |
|                                   | In Customer First:                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Search Fast Note in Workspace |
|                                   | -   Enter 'ESAt' or 'ESAt         |
|                                   |     referral' into the text box   |
|                                   |     and select the Search button  |
|                                   | -   Select template ESAt          |
|                                   |     Appointment Required          |
|                                   | -   Once the text has been        |
|                                   |     confirmed update all the      |
|                                   |     fields in the text to reflect |
|                                   |     circumstances, include        |
|                                   |     information of ESAt finalised |
|                                   |     on Multiple CRN and           |
|                                   |     requirement for an ESAt file  |
|                                   |     assessment is completed on    |
|                                   |     Primary CRN                   |
|                                   | -   Leave the Fast Note open, it  |
|                                   |     does not need to be           |
|                                   |     transferred out or            |
|                                   |     re-categorised as this will   |
|                                   |     occur automatically           |
|                                   | -   See Table 5                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, see Table 5                   |

Customer linked to Multiple Record Partner

Table 4

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Locate the customer record and    |
|                                   | confirm relationship start date + |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Using the information provided in |
|                                   | the DQU ACTDOC, locate the        |
|                                   | customer record that is linked to |
|                                   | a multiple record.                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the Marital Status (MS)     |
|                                   | screen and confirm the            |
|                                   | relationship start date.          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Unlink the partner and finalise   |
|                                   | activity + Read more ...          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the MS screen, unlink the      |
|                                   | partner from their relationship   |
|                                   | start date by deleting the        |
|                                   | relationship status line          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices:                  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   From the Assessment Results   |
|                                   |     (AR) screen, go to the        |
|                                   |     Assessment Consequences (ASC) |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   In the Letter Action: field,  |
|                                   |     code 'INH'                    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If arrears generate from deleting |
|                                   | the relationship link:            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the AR screen           |
|                                   | -   From the Daily Rate Summary   |
|                                   |     (RATS) screen, go to the      |
|                                   |     Customer Daily Rate Component |
|                                   |     (RAC) screen                  |
|                                   | -   Code Manual Adjustment: 0     |
|                                   | -   Code Manual Adjustment        |
|                                   |     reason: ADJ - Adjustment      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Finalise the activity             |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Link to the Primary Partner       |
|                                   | record + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to the MS screen to link the   |
|                                   | primary partner record from the   |
|                                   | relevant start date               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Code a new relationship       |
|                                   |     status line on the MS screen. |
|                                   |     See Table 2 in Change in      |
|                                   |     relationship status from      |
|                                   |     single to partnered           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If an overpayment occurs:         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   From the RATS screen, go to   |
|                                   |     the RAC screen                |
|                                   | -   Code Manual Adjustment: 0     |
|                                   | -   Code Manual Adjustment        |
|                                   |     reason: ADJ - Adjustment      |
|                                   | -   Ensure the overpayment amount |
|                                   |     is 0 for the same period the  |
|                                   |     arrears were 0 for            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Inhibit advices                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   From the AR screen, go to the |
|                                   |     ASC screen                    |
|                                   | -   In Letter Action: field, code |
|                                   |     'INH'                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Table 5.                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Nominee Action

Table 5

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Customer has nominee              |
|                                   | arrangement + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is there a nominee arrangement    |
|                                   | recorded on the customer's        |
|                                   | multiple CRN?                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, see Table 6               |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | End Multiple CRN Nominee          |
|                                   | Arrangement + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Manually code the nominee         |
|                                   | cancellation.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In the customer's record, select  |
|                                   | the nominee arrangement from the  |
|                                   | Customer Link Summary (NOLS)      |
|                                   | screen. The Nominee Task Selector |
|                                   | (NOTS) screen will be displayed   |
|                                   | in the nominee's record:          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Select the Nominee Relationship   |
|                                   | Summary (NORS) screen             |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   In the Date of effect field,  |
|                                   |     key the date the arrangement  |
|                                   |     is to end. If this field is   |
|                                   |     coded, the reason field must  |
|                                   |     also be keyed                 |
|                                   | -   In the End Reason field, key  |
|                                   |     CNV - Conversion. Using this  |
|                                   |     code will not issue a         |
|                                   |     cancellation letter to the    |
|                                   |     customer and the nominee      |
|                                   | -   in the Action field, key an   |
|                                   |     'I' for Insert                |
|                                   | -   complete the footer details   |
|                                   |     using internal (INT) for      |
|                                   |     Source and today's date for   |
|                                   |     Date of receipt (DOR) press   |
|                                   |     [Enter]                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Recording these fields will end   |
|                                   | the link between the nominee and  |
|                                   | the customer.                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | On the customer's record, DOC     |
|                                   | details that the cancellation is  |
|                                   | the result of DQU remediation     |
|                                   | work and needing to link nominee  |
|                                   | to primary CRN.                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If there is a Display on Access   |
|                                   | DOC about the nominee             |
|                                   | arrangement, expire the DOC.      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Determine type of Nominee         |
|                                   | Arrangement for Primary CRN +     |
|                                   | Read more ...                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Refer to the Authorising a person |
|                                   | or organisation to enquire or act |
|                                   | on your behalf (SS313) form       |
|                                   | transferred to Primary CRN.       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Determine the type of nominee     |
|                                   | arrangement:                      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Correspondence nominee or     |
|                                   |     both Correspondence & Payment |
|                                   |     nominee, go to Step 4         |
|                                   | -   Payment nominee only, go to   |
|                                   |     Step 6                        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Correspondence and both           |
|                                   | Correspondence & Payment Nominee  |
|                                   | Arrangement + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | In Customer Record, is the        |
|                                   | Nominee Action Script available?  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, use the Nominee Action       |
|                                   | script in Customer Record to      |
|                                   | record a new Nominee authority    |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Ensure both nominee arrangements  |
|                                   | are recorded if payment and       |
|                                   | correspondence nominee            |
|                                   | arrangements are requested        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the message 'Do you wish to    |
|                                   | send Appointment of Nominee       |
|                                   | letters (Y/N)?' presents, select  |
|                                   | Y. It is important that both the  |
|                                   | customer and the nominee are      |
|                                   | advised that the arrangement has  |
|                                   | been recorded on the correct CRN  |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The following actions may also be |
|                                   | required after the script has     |
|                                   | completed:                        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   for involuntary arrangements, |
|                                   |     the Display on Access DOC     |
|                                   |     will need to be annotated,    |
|                                   |     with the following            |
|                                   |     information: 'Involuntary     |
|                                   |     <correspondence/payment>      |
|                                   |     nominee arrangements. Do not  |
|                                   |     grant advance or urgent       |
|                                   |     payments, create or vary      |
|                                   |     deductions, cancel nominee    |
|                                   |     arrangement, change payment   |
|                                   |     destination or update rent or |
|                                   |     assets without contacting     |
|                                   |     nominee and obtaining         |
|                                   |     approval'                     |
|                                   | -   document number, if provided  |
|                                   | -   mail suppression will need to |
|                                   |     be coded for an involuntary   |
|                                   |     arrangement, if required      |
|                                   | -   organisation reference        |
|                                   |     number, if required           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, if the script is unavailable: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Add a new nominee link by     |
|                                   |     completing the Add New Link:  |
|                                   |     PER/ORG:, NOM TYPE: NOC/NOP   |
|                                   |     and DOE: fields on the NOLS   |
|                                   |     screen                        |
|                                   | -   If the new nominee is a       |
|                                   |     person, the Name Search (IN)  |
|                                   |     screen displays service       |
|                                   |     reason NOM and action NLK, or |
|                                   |     if the new nominee is an      |
|                                   |     organisation, the             |
|                                   |     Organisation Name Search (ON) |
|                                   |     screen displays service       |
|                                   |     reason NOM and action NLK     |
|                                   | -   Select the Nominee            |
|                                   |     Relationship Summary (NORS)   |
|                                   |     screen and enter all details  |
|                                   | -   Password must be recorded     |
|                                   | -   Relationship to customer is   |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   Reason for arrangement is     |
|                                   |     required                      |
|                                   | -   End date of nominee           |
|                                   |     arrangement should be         |
|                                   |     recorded if requested         |
|                                   | -   Document number is optional,  |
|                                   |     but should be recorded if     |
|                                   |     provided                      |
|                                   | -   Mail suppression, if the      |
|                                   |     arrangement is involuntary    |
|                                   |     and the nominee has requested |
|                                   |     that mail be suppressed to    |
|                                   |     the customer                  |
|                                   | -   Organisation reference number |
|                                   |     is optional                   |
|                                   | -   If the message 'Do you wish   |
|                                   |     to send Appointment of        |
|                                   |     Nominee letters (Y/N)?'       |
|                                   |     presents, select Y. It is     |
|                                   |     important that both the       |
|                                   |     customer and the nominee are  |
|                                   |     advised that the arrangement  |
|                                   |     has been recorded on the      |
|                                   |     correct CRN                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the nominee arrangement is     |
|                                   | involuntary, for example it is    |
|                                   | appointed by the court,           |
|                                   | Guardianship Board or             |
|                                   | Administrative Tribunal and the   |
|                                   | nominee has requested that no     |
|                                   | correspondence is to be received  |
|                                   | by the customer, select the       |
|                                   | Suppress Advices to Customer      |
|                                   | option.                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Go to Step 5 for additional       |
|                                   | coding if required to finalise    |
|                                   | the payment nominee arrangement   |
|                                   | part for a nominee that is both   |
|                                   | payment and correspondence        |
|                                   | nominee.                          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 5                                 | Additional coding required to     |
|                                   | finalise the payment nominee part |
|                                   | for a nominee arrangement that is |
|                                   | for both payment and              |
|                                   | correspondence nominee + Read     |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For payment nominee arrangement,  |
|                                   | continue with the following       |
|                                   | manual coding in the nominee      |
|                                   | activity:                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Record payment destination        |
|                                   | details:                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   If the existing payment       |
|                                   |     destination is correct on the |
|                                   |     Nominee Destination Summary   |
|                                   |     (NODS) screen, code 'L'       |
|                                   |     beside the existing payment   |
|                                   |     destination, press [Enter]    |
|                                   |     and code 'Y' in the Confirm   |
|                                   |     link: field                   |
|                                   | -   If the payment nominee's      |
|                                   |     payment destination is a      |
|                                   |     group payment, ensure the     |
|                                   |     customer's record is in the   |
|                                   |     same environment where the    |
|                                   |     nominee organisation is       |
|                                   |     situated. The Resources page  |
|                                   |     of Appointing nominees has    |
|                                   |     examples of when to transfer  |
|                                   |     a record due to a group       |
|                                   |     payment arrangement. For the  |
|                                   |     transfer process, see         |
|                                   |     Inter-environment change of   |
|                                   |     address (ICoA) of a customer  |
|                                   |     record using Customer First   |
|                                   |     or Customer Record            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To add a new payment destination: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the NODS screen, enter  |
|                                   |     'Y' in the Add new payment    |
|                                   |     destination: field and press  |
|                                   |     [Enter]                       |
|                                   | -   On the Nominee Payment        |
|                                   |     Destination Details (NODD)    |
|                                   |     screen, enter details of the  |
|                                   |     Direct Credit account         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a DOC stating type of      |
|                                   | nominee arrangement. If the       |
|                                   | arrangement is involuntary,       |
|                                   | ensure the DOC is Display on      |
|                                   | Access (DOA). Include this text   |
|                                   | in the DOA DOC: 'Involuntary      |
|                                   | <correspondence/payment> nominee  |
|                                   | arrangements. Do not grant        |
|                                   | advance or urgent payments,       |
|                                   | create or vary deductions, cancel |
|                                   | nominee arrangement, change       |
|                                   | payment destination or update     |
|                                   | rent or assets without contacting |
|                                   | nominee and obtaining approval'   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the nominee arrangement is     |
|                                   | involuntary, for example it is    |
|                                   | appointed by the court,           |
|                                   | Guardianship Board or             |
|                                   | Administrative Tribunal and the   |
|                                   | nominee has requested that no     |
|                                   | correspondence is to be received  |
|                                   | by the customer, select the       |
|                                   | Suppress Advices to Customer      |
|                                   | option.                           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

|                                   | ensure the customer's record is   |
|                                   | in the same environment where the |
|                                   | nominee organisation is situated. |
|                                   | The Resources page of Appointing  |
|                                   | nominees has examples of when to  |
|                                   | transfer a record due to a group  |
|                                   | payment arrangement. For the      |
|                                   | transfer process, see             |
|                                   | Inter-environment change of       |
|                                   | address (ICoA) of a customer      |
|                                   | record using Customer First or    |
|                                   | Customer Record                   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | To add a new payment destination: |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Go to the NODS screen, enter  |
|                                   |     'Y' in the Add new payment    |
|                                   |     destination: field and press  |
|                                   |     [Enter]                       |
|                                   | -   On the Nominee Payment        |
|                                   |     Destination Details (NODD)    |
|                                   |     screen, enter details of the  |
|                                   |     Direct Credit account         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Create a DOC stating type of      |
|                                   | nominee arrangement. If the       |
|                                   | arrangement is involuntary,       |
|                                   | ensure the DOC is Display on      |
|                                   | Access (DOA). Include this text   |
|                                   | in the DOA DOC: 'Involuntary      |
|                                   | <correspondence/payment> nominee  |
|                                   | arrangements. Do not grant        |
|                                   | advance or urgent payments,       |
|                                   | create or vary deductions, cancel |
|                                   | nominee arrangement, change       |
|                                   | payment destination or update     |
|                                   | rent or assets without contacting |
|                                   | nominee and obtaining approval'   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the nominee arrangement is     |
|                                   | involuntary for example, it is    |
|                                   | appointed by the court,           |
|                                   | Guardianship Board or             |
|                                   | Administrative Tribunal and the   |
|                                   | nominee has requested that no     |
|                                   | correspondence is to be received  |
|                                   | by the customer, select the       |
|                                   | Suppress Advices to Customer      |
|                                   | option.                           |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 7                                 | Self Service for Nominees + Read  |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the nominee arrangement is for |
|                                   | an:                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Individual, go to Step 8      |
|                                   | -   Organisation, go to Step 9    |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 8                                 | Individual Nominee - Self Service |
|                                   | Contact + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | For individual nominees, a        |
|                                   | pre-call notification SMS via     |
|                                   | Desktop Messaging must be sent.   |
|                                   | See Desktop (DEMC) Messages on    |
|                                   | the Resources page.               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make a genuine attempt to contact |
|                                   | the nominee to advise the nominee |
|                                   | arrangement was transferred to    |
|                                   | their principal's Primary CRN and |
|                                   | to discuss self-service, if       |
|                                   | required.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the nominee currently          |
|                                   | registered for online services as |
|                                   | a customer?                       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Yes, go to Step 10                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | No, advise the nominee of the     |
|                                   | benefits of online services       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Once registered for a         |
|                                   |     Centrelink online account and |
|                                   |     nominee online services, the  |
|                                   |     nominee will have access to   |
|                                   |     any new nominee arrangements  |
|                                   |     via their online account      |
|                                   | -   To register, the nominee      |
|                                   |     needs to create a myGov       |
|                                   |     account and link Centrelink   |
|                                   |     services to it. For more      |
|                                   |     information, see Access to    |
|                                   |     Centrelink self service - set |
|                                   |     up, checking, locking and     |
|                                   |     resetting                     |
|                                   | -   Service Officers can register |
|                                   |     nominees via Access           |
|                                   |     Management for Self Service   |
|                                   |     (AMSS). The nominee can       |
|                                   |     register online themselves    |
|                                   |     for nominee online services   |
|                                   | -   See Table 6                   |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 9                                 | Organisation Nominee - Self       |
|                                   | Service + Read more ...           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Make a genuine attempt to contact |
|                                   | the nominee to advise the nominee |
|                                   | arrangement was transferred to    |
|                                   | their principal's Primary CRN and |
|                                   | to discuss self-service, if       |
|                                   | required.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The nominee organisation's        |
|                                   | contact details can be found on   |
|                                   | the Organisation Contact Summary  |
|                                   | (OSCS) screen in the nominee's    |
|                                   | record. Select the contact person |
|                                   | to display the phone number.      |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the nominee currently          |
|                                   | registered with Business Hub for  |
|                                   | organisation nominee online       |
|                                   | services?                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, see Step 1 in Table 6    |
|                                   | -   No, advise the nominee of the |
|                                   |     benefits of online services.  |
|                                   |     To register for Business Hub  |
|                                   |     and organisation nominee      |
|                                   |     online services, see Online   |
|                                   |     Services for organisation     |
|                                   |     nominees                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 10                                | Check registration for nominee    |
|                                   | online services + Read more ...   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The nominee may need to           |
|                                   | re-register for nominee online    |
|                                   | services, if their principal is   |
|                                   | the only person they are nominee  |
|                                   | for.                              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Service Officers can register     |
|                                   | nominees via Access Management    |
|                                   | for Self Service (AMSS). The      |
|                                   | nominee can register online       |
|                                   | themselves for nominee online     |
|                                   | services.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | See Table 6.                      |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+

Unlink and relink Centrelink online account

Table 6

+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| Step                              | Action                            |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 1                                 | Check the Manage Self Service     |
|                                   | Access screen on the multiple     |
|                                   | record + Read more ...            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Is the Web Access Channel Status  |
|                                   | locked?                           |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 2             |
|                                   | -   No, use the Change access     |
|                                   |     status tab and select Lock    |
|                                   |     Password. Go to Step 2        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 2                                 | Contact the customer + Read more  |
|                                   | ...                               |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Prior to contacting the customer  |
|                                   | by phone, a pre-call notification |
|                                   | SMS via Desktop Messaging must be |
|                                   | sent. See Desktop (DEMC) Messages |
|                                   | on the Resources page.            |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Call and authenticate the         |
|                                   | customer.                         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Advise the customer:              |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   a second Centrelink record    |
|                                   |     was incorrectly created       |
|                                   | -   all their information has now |
|                                   |     moved from the new record to  |
|                                   |     the existing record           |
|                                   | -   their myGov account is        |
|                                   |     currently linked to their     |
|                                   |     incorrect record and the call |
|                                   |     is to help them to fix this   |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | If the customer states they are   |
|                                   | suspicious of the call, advise    |
|                                   | they can call back and provide    |
|                                   | their identity information to     |
|                                   | receive a linking code. The       |
|                                   | Resources page has a link to the  |
|                                   | agency's contact details.         |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Advise the customer they will     |
|                                   | need to unlink the Centrelink     |
|                                   | Service to be able to use the     |
|                                   | linking code to re-link to their  |
|                                   | Primary record CRN. If this       |
|                                   | occurs, update the ACTDOC.        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Was the customer contacted        |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Yes, go to Step 3             |
|                                   | -   No, after 2 unsuccessful      |
|                                   |     contacts, go to Step 4        |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 3                                 | Run the myGov Staff Linking       |
|                                   | Application + Read more ...       |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   Select the Centrelink box and |
|                                   |     enter the customer's primary  |
|                                   |     record CRN. Select Continue   |
|                                   | -   Confirm the Customer's name,  |
|                                   |     Date of birth and Address,    |
|                                   |     and ask if they have a photo  |
|                                   |     ID document to Fast Track the |
|                                   |     process. Select Yes or No,    |
|                                   |     then Continue                 |
|                                   | -   Complete either the Fast      |
|                                   |     Track process or the Question |
|                                   |     and Answer process and        |
|                                   |     generate the Linking Code     |
|                                   | -   Provide the linking code and  |
|                                   |     the Primary CRN to the        |
|                                   |     customer                      |
|                                   | -   Advise the customer to sign   |
|                                   |     in to their myGov account and |
|                                   |     select Services and Unlink    |
|                                   |     Centrelink. Confirm the       |
|                                   |     unlink message                |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer will be returned to  |
|                                   | the Services, Link a service page |
|                                   | where they can select Centrelink  |
|                                   | and choose I have a linking code. |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | The customer can enter the        |
|                                   | linking code and their primary    |
|                                   | record CRN to link their correct  |
|                                   | Centrelink record to their myGov  |
|                                   | account.                          |
+-----------------------------------+-----------------------------------+
| 4                                 | Update the Multiple Record + Read |
|                                   | more ...                          |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Annotate the DOC to record the    |
|                                   | customer was:                     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | -   successfully contacted or     |
|                                   |     unsuccessfully contacted      |
|                                   | -   issued a new linking code,    |
|                                   |     and                           |
|                                   | -   told how to unlink/relink     |
|                                   |                                   |
|                                   | Complete the ACTDOC if all other  |
|                                   | multiple record remediation work  |
|                                   | is complete.                      |
